  <script type="text/javascript">
   /**
		 * Wrapper for HTML5 WebStorage
		 *
		 * BB.localStorage.set('foo', {bar:[1,2]});
		 * BB.sessionStorage.get('foo');
		 * BB.localStorage.rm('foo');
		 */
		$.each(['localStorage', 'sessionStorage'], function (i, type) {
			BB[type] = {
				supported: !!window[type],
				get: function (key) {
					if (!this.supported) {
						return null;
					}
					var val_str = window[type].getItem(key);
					var val_orig = JSON.parse(val_str);
					return val_orig;
				},
				set: function (key, value) {
					if (this.supported) {
						try {
							var val_str = JSON.stringify(value);
							window[type].setItem(key, val_str);
						} catch (e)
						{}
					}
				},
				rm: function (key) {
					if (this.supported) {
						window[type].removeItem(key);
					}
				}
			};
		});

		var BB_ROOT      = "./";
		var cookieDomain = ".uraltrack.net";
		var cookiePath   = "/";
		var cookiePrefix = "bb_";
		var cookieSecure = 0;
		var LOGGED_IN    = 0;
		var IWP          = 'HEIGHT=510,WIDTH=780,resizable=yes';
		var IWP_US       = 'HEIGHT=250,WIDTH=400,resizable=yes';
		var IWP_SM       = 'HEIGHT=420,WIDTH=470,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes';

		var user = {
			opt_js: {},

			set: function (opt, val, days, reload) {
				this.opt_js[opt] = val;
				setCookie('opt_js', $.toJSON(this.opt_js), days);
				if (reload) {
					window.location.reload();
				}
			}
		};

		
		var ajax = new Ajax('http://uraltrack.net/ajax.php', 'POST', 'json');

		function getElText(e) {
			var t = '';
			if (e.textContent !== undefined) {
				t = e.textContent;
			} else if (e.innerText !== undefined) {
				t = e.innerText;
			} else {
				t = jQuery(e).text();
			}
			return t;
		}
		function escHTML(txt) {
			return txt.replace(/</g, '&lt;');
		}
		
		function cfm(txt) {
			return window.confirm(txt);
		}
		function bb_alert(txt, is_error) {
			var html = txt.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
			$('#bb-alert-msg').html(html);
			$('#bb-alert-box').toggleClass('bb-alert-err', is_error == true).jsmodal();
			return false;
		}
		function post2url(url, params) {
			params = params || {};
			var f = document.createElement('form');
			f.setAttribute('method', 'post');
			f.setAttribute('action', url);
			params['form_token'] = '';
			for (var k in params) {
				var h = document.createElement('input');
				h.setAttribute('type', 'hidden');
				h.setAttribute('name', k);
				h.setAttribute('value', params[k]);
				f.appendChild(h);
			}
			document.body.appendChild(f);
			f.submit();
			return false;
		}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function () {
		$('#cse-search-btn, #cse-search-btn-top').click(function () {
			var text_match_input_id = $(this).attr('href');
			var text_match = $('#' + text_match_input_id).val();
			if (text_match == '') {
				$('#' + text_match_input_id).addClass('hl-err-block').focus();
				return false;
			}
			$('#cse-text-match').val(text_match);
			$('#cse-submit-btn').click();
			return false;
		});

		$('#search-action').bind('change', function () {
			if ($('#search-text').val() != '') {
				$('#quick-search input[type="submit"]').prop({disabled: true});
				$('#quick-search').submit();
			}
		});

		$('#quick-search').submit(function () {
			var action = $('#search-action').val();
			var txt = $('#search-text').val();
			$(this).attr('target', '');
			if (txt == 'поиск...' || txt == '') {
				$('#search-text').val('').addClass('hl-err-block').focus();
				return false;
			}
			if (action == 'hash') {
				window.location.href = 'viewtopic.php?h=' + txt;
				return false;
			}
			else {
				$(this).attr('action', action);
			}
		});
	});
  </script>

               function set_h_cat() {
										h_cats = [];
										$.each($('input.h-cat-cbx:checked'), function (i, el) {
											h_cats.push($(this).val());
										});
